                <h3 class="title-about">Quienes somos?</h3>
                <p class="about-text">MAXICAMBIOS inició sus actividades en el mercado de cambios del Paraguay
                    el 16 de mayo de 2003, bajo la razón social de MAXICAMBIOS S.A.</p>
                <ul class="nav nav-tabs" style="border:0!important;">
                                                            <li id="active-init" class=""><a id="active-init-a" class="" data-toggle="tab" href="#menu1" aria-expanded="true">Misión</a></li>
                                                                                <li id="active-init" class=""><a id="active-init-a" class="" data-toggle="tab" href="#menu4" aria-expanded="true">Visión</a></li>
                                                                                <li id="active-init" class=""><a id="active-init-a" class="" data-toggle="tab" href="#menu5" aria-expanded="true">Valores</a></li>
                                                                                <li id="active-init" class=""><a id="active-init-a" class="" data-toggle="tab" href="#menu3" aria-expanded="true">Perfil</a></li>
                                                                                <li id="active-init" class=""><a id="active-init-a" class="" data-toggle="tab" href="#menu2" aria-expanded="true">Autorización</a></li>
                                                        </ul>
                <div class="tab-content">
                                                                <div id="menu1" class="tab-pane fade active-init-description ">
                            <p>
                                Brindar soluciones en el mercado de cambios y servicios con agilidad y responsabilidad, asegurando la satisfacción de clientes, aliados y colaboradores.
                            </p>
                        </div>
                                                                                    <div id="menu4" class="tab-pane fade active-init-description ">
                            <p>
                                Seremos innovadores, generando alianzas de valor.
                            </p>
                        </div>
                                                                                    <div id="menu5" class="tab-pane fade active-init-description ">
                            <p>
                                - Honestidad
- Profesionalismo
- Humildad
- Respeto
- Responsabilidad
- Lealtad
- Compromiso
- Confianza
                            </p>
                        </div>
                                                                                    <div id="menu3" class="tab-pane fade active-init-description ">
                            <p>
                                La empresa tiene como principal actividad la prestación de servicios cambiarios y pago de servicios a empresas y personas físicas.
                            </p>
                        </div>

            $(document).on('ajaxSetup', function(event, context) {
                // Handle Error Messages with a custom handler
                context.options.handleErrorMessage = function(message) {
                    const Toast = Swal.mixin({
                        toast: true,
                        position: 'top-end',
                        showConfirmButton: false,
                        timer: 3000,
                        timerProgressBar: true,
                        onOpen: (toast) => {
                        toast.addEventListener('mouseenter', Swal.stopTimer)
                        toast.addEventListener('mouseleave', Swal.resumeTimer)
                        }
                    })

                    Toast.fire({
                        icon: 'error',
                        title: message
                    })

                    $( document ).ready(function() {
                        $('form').each(function() { this.reset() });
                    });
                }

                // Handle Flash Messages with a custom handler
                context.options.handleFlashMessage = function(message, type) {
                    const Toast = Swal.mixin({
                        toast: true,
                        position: 'top-end',
                        showConfirmButton: false,
                        timer: 3000,
                        timerProgressBar: true,
                        onOpen: (toast) => {
                        toast.addEventListener('mouseenter', Swal.stopTimer)
                        toast.addEventListener('mouseleave', Swal.resumeTimer)
                        }
                    })

                    Toast.fire({
                        icon: 'success',
                        title: message
                    })

                    $( document ).ready(function() {
                        $('form').each(function() { this.reset() });
                    });
                }
            })

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).ready(function(){
          $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();

          mapLoad();

        });

        var acc = document.getElementsByClassName("well-accordion");
        var i;

        for (i = 0; i < acc.length; i++) {
          acc[i].addEventListener("click", function() {
            /* Toggle between adding and removing the "active" class,
            to highlight the button that controls the panel */
            this.classList.toggle("active");

            /* Toggle between hiding and showing the active panel */
            var panel = this.nextElementSibling;
            if (panel.style.display === "block") {
              panel.style.display = "none";
            } else {
              panel.style.display = "block";
            }
          });
        }

        function mapLoad(){
          $(this).request('onCiudadFilter', {
            data: {
              ciudad_id: 0,
            },
            update: {'public/_list_offices.htm':'#form_refresh_on'},
          });

          setTimeout(function(){
              $('#offices-all').addClass('disabled');
              initMap();
          }, 500);

          $("#ciudad_id").prop('selectedIndex',0);
        }

        function initMap(){

          const position = [-25.3165968, -57.7215786];
          const map = L.map('map',
            {
            scrollWheelZoom: false
            }
          ).setView(position, 10);

          L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.osm.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
            attribution: '&copy; <a href="https://osm.org/copyright">OpenStreetMap</a> contributors'
          }).addTo(map);

          var myIcon = L.icon({
              iconUrl: 'https://www.maxicambios.com.py/themes/maxicambios_2/assets/images/flaticon_map.png',
              iconSize: [40, 40],
              popupAnchor: [-3, -20],
          });

                      L.marker([-25.3166893, -57.571653200000014], {icon: myIcon})
            .addTo(map)
            .bindPopup('<div id="content">'+
              '<div id="bodyContent" style-"max-width:40vh;">'+
              '<div class="row">'+
              '<div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12" style="text-align:center;">'+
              '<img src="https://www.maxicambios.com.py/storage/app/uploads/public/5d6/ffe/0b9/5d6ffe0b93019070535960.jpg" style="max-height:60%;max-width:50%;"/>'+
              '</div><div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12">'+
              '<p style="color:black;">Shopping Multiplaza Casa Central</p>'+
              '</div></div>'+
              '<div class="row">'+
              '<div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12 text-center">'+
              '<a href="https://www.google.com/maps?q=-25.3166893,-57.571653200000014" target="_blank">Ver en Maps</a>'+
              '</div></div></div><br/>'+
              '</div>')
            .closePopup();
                      L.marker([-25.3259849, -57.59602240000004], {icon: myIcon})
            .addTo(map)
            .bindPopup('<div id="content">'+
              '<div id="bodyContent" style-"max-width:40vh;">'+
              '<div class="row">'+
              '<div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12" style="text-align:center;">'+
              '<img src="https://www.maxicambios.com.py/storage/app/uploads/public/644/bd3/248/644bd324836e5121752154.jpeg" style="max-height:60%;max-width:50%;"/>'+
              '</div><div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12">'+
              '<p style="color:black;">Terminal de Omnibus</p>'+
              '</div></div>'+
              '<div class="row">'+
              '<div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12 text-center">'+
              '<a href="https://www.google.com/maps?q=-25.3259849,-57.59602240000004" target="_blank">Ver en Maps</a>'+
              '</div></div></div><br/>'+
              '</div>')

              '<div id="bodyContent" style-"max-width:40vh;">'+

        function initMap2(latitud, longitud, zoom, sucursal) {

            document.getElementById('map_container').innerHTML = "<div id='map' style='height: 40.0em;border-radius: 15px;'></div>";

            const position = [latitud, longitud];
            const map = L.map('map').setView(position, 16);

            L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.osm.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
              attribution: '&copy; <a href="https://osm.org/copyright">OpenStreetMap</a> contributors'
            }).addTo(map);

            var myIcon = L.icon({
                iconUrl: 'https://www.maxicambios.com.py/themes/maxicambios_2/assets/images/flaticon_map.png',
                iconSize: [40, 40],
                popupAnchor: [-3, -20],
            });

            if (sucursal) {
                var title = sucursal['name'] ? sucursal['name'] : 'Sin nombre';
                var image = sucursal['photo'] ? sucursal['photo']['path'] : "https://www.maxicambios.com.py/themes/default/assets/images/about-us.png";
                var latitud = sucursal['latlon']['latitud'];
                var longitud = sucursal['latlon']['longitud'];

                L.marker([latitud, longitud],16, {icon: myIcon})
                .addTo(map)
                .bindPopup('<div id="content">'+
                  '<div id="bodyContent" style-"max-width:40vh;">'+
                  '<div class="row">'+
                  '<div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12" style="text-align:center;">'+
                  '<img src="'+image+'" style="max-height:60%;max-width:50%;"/>'+
                  '</div><div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12">'+
                  '<p style="color:black;">'+title+'</p>'+
                  '</div></div>'+
                  '<div class="row">'+
                  '<div class="col-lg-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-xs-12 text-center">'+
                  '<a href="https://www.google.com/maps?q='+latitud+','+longitud+'" target="_blank">Ver en Maps</a>'+
                  '</div></div></div><br/>'+
                  '</div>')
                .openPopup();
            }
            $('#offices-all').removeClass('disabled');
        }

        function mapReload() {

          document.getElementById('map_container').innerHTML = "<div id='map' style='height: 40.0em;border-radius: 15px;'></div>";

          initMap();

        }

<script type="text/javascript">

    $("#whatsapp").on("click", function() {

        var item = document.getElementById("wp_admin");

        if(item.classList.contains('maxi-show')){
            $(".maxi-container").removeClass("maxi-show");
        }else{
            $(".maxi-container").addClass("maxi-show");
        }

    });

</script>
<script type="text/javascript">

    var q = 0;
    var x_timer;
    var url_image;
    var start = new Date();
    var previusDay = new Date(start);
        previusDay.setDate(start.getDate()-100);

    $('#submit_history').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        try {
            //Screen html
            var canvas = document.getElementById("myChart");
            var img = canvas.toDataURL("image/png");

            url_image = img;
        } catch (err) {
            console.error(err);
        }

        $('#shareHistory').addClass('hidden');
        $('.modal-backdrop').addClass('hidden')
        $('#share_button_text').addClass('hidden');
        $('#share_button_text_loading').removeClass('hidden');
        $('#share_history').request('onShareHistory', {
            data:{
                email: $('#email_history').val(),
                na: $('select[name="na"]').val(),
                data_init: $('input[name="data_inicio"]').val(),
                data_finish: $('input[name="data_fin"]').val(),
                image: url_image,
            },
            success: function (data) {
                const Toast = Swal.mixin({
                    toast: true,
                    position: 'top-end',
                    showConfirmButton: false,
                    timer: 4000,
                    timerProgressBar: true,
                    onOpen: (toast) => {
                    toast.addEventListener('mouseenter', Swal.stopTimer)
                    toast.addEventListener('mouseleave', Swal.resumeTimer)
                    }
                });

                Toast.fire({
                    icon: 'success',
                    title: 'Enviado correctamente. Gracias.'
                });

                $('#share_button_text_loading').addClass('hidden');
                $('#share_button_text').removeClass('hidden');
            },
            fail: function (data) {
                const Toast = Swal.mixin({
                    toast: true,
                    position: 'top-end',
                    showConfirmButton: false,
                    timer: 4000,
                    timerProgressBar: true,
                    onOpen: (toast) => {
                    toast.addEventListener('mouseenter', Swal.stopTimer)
                    toast.addEventListener('mouseleave', Swal.resumeTimer)
                    }
                });

                Toast.fire({
                    icon: 'error',
                    title: 'Ocurrio un error. Intentelo de nuevo.'
                });

                $('#share_button_text_loading').addClass('hidden');
                $('#share_button_text').removeClass('hidden');
            }
        });
    });

    function CopyHtml() {

        var getUrl = window.location;
        var baseUrl = getUrl.protocol + "//" + getUrl.host + "/" + getUrl.pathname.split('/')[1];

        var link = baseUrl + "/share";

        var dummyContent = "<iframe src=\"" + link + "\" width=\"100%\" height=\"100%\"></iframe>";
        var dummy = $('<input>').val(dummyContent).appendTo('#button-share').select();
        document.execCommand('copy');
    }

    $(function() {

        new AutoNumeric('#importe', {
            decimalCharacter : ',',
            digitGroupSeparator : '.',
        });

        new AutoNumeric('#segundo_valor', {
            decimalCharacter : ',',
            digitGroupSeparator : '.',
        });

        var day = new Date();
        var previusDay = new Date(day);
        previusDay.setDate(day.getDate()-100);

        $(".site-navigation-mobile").css({
            overflow:'hidden'
        });
        $('.site-navigation-mobile').off('mousedown', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
        });

        $('input[name="data_inicio"]').datepicker({
            onSelect: function (fd, d, picker) {
                $('#chart-form').request('onHistoricoPartial');
            }
        });
        $('input[name="data_fin"]').datepicker({
            onSelect: function (fd, d, picker) {
                $('#chart-form').request('onHistoricoPartial');
            }
        });

        $(".site-navigation-mobile").css({
            overflow:'hidden'
        });
        $('.site-navigation-mobile').off('mousedown', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
        });

        var asuncion_xs = $('#asuncion_xs');
        asuncion_xs.css('background-color', '#eee');

        $('input[name="data_inicio"]').datepicker({
            dateFormat: 'dd-mm-yyyy',
        }).data('datepicker').selectDate(previusDay);
        $('input[name="data_fin"]').datepicker({
            dateFormat: 'dd-mm-yyyy',
        }).data('datepicker').selectDate(start);

        // Form submit on load page.
        $('#chart-form').request('onHistoricoPartial');

        $('#calculadora-search').request('onCalculadora', {
            data:{
                moneda_origen: $('#moneda_origen').val(),
                importe: parseInt($('#importe').val()),
                moneda_destino: $('#moneda_destino').val(),
                search: '0',
            },
        });
    });

    var importe = $('#importe');
    var form_calculator = $('#bitcoin-calculator');
    var o_moneda = $('#moneda_origen');
    var d_moneda = $('#moneda_destino');
    var loader_gif = $("#loader-calculate");
    var segundo_valor = $('#segundo_valor');

    (function($) {
    $.fn.donetyping = function(callback){
        var _this = $(this);
        _this.keyup(function (){
            clearTimeout(x_timer);
            x_timer = setTimeout(clear_timer, 1500);
        });

        function clear_timer(){
            clearTimeout(x_timer);
            callback.call(_this);
        }
    }
    })(jQuery);

    function charSelect(){

        $('#chart-form').request('onHistoricoPartial');
    }

    function oneSelect(){

        var importe_parse = parseFloat($('#importe').val().replace(/[.\/#!$%\^&\*;:{}=\-_`~()]/g,''));

        $('#calculadora-search').request('onCalculadora', {
            data:{
                moneda_origen: $('#moneda_origen').val(),
                importe: importe_parse,
                moneda_destino: $('#moneda_destino').val(),
                search: '0'
            },
        });

        loader_gif.removeClass('hidden');
        loader_gif.addClass('active');
        o_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
        d_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
        $('#importe').prop('disabled', true);
        $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', true);

        setTimeout(function(){
            loader_gif.removeClass('active');
            loader_gif.addClass('hidden');
            o_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
            d_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
            $('#importe').prop('disabled', false);
            $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', false);
        }, 2000);
    };

    function twoSelect(){

        var importe_parse = parseFloat($('#importe').val().replace(/[.\/#!$%\^&\*;:{}=\-_`~()]/g,''));
        var segundo_valor_parse = parseFloat($('#segundo_valor').val().replace(/[.\/#!$%\^&\*;:{}=\-_`~()]/g,''));

        $('#calculadora-search').request('onCalculadora', {
            data:{
                moneda_origen: $('#moneda_origen').val(),
                importe: importe_parse,
                segundo_valor: segundo_valor_parse,
                moneda_destino: $('#moneda_destino').val(),
                search: '0',
            },
        });

        loader_gif.removeClass('hidden');
        loader_gif.addClass('active');
        o_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
        d_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
        $('#importe').prop('disabled', true);
        $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', true);

        setTimeout(function(){
            loader_gif.removeClass('active');
            loader_gif.addClass('hidden');
            o_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
            d_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
            $('#importe').prop('disabled', false);
            $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', false);
        }, 2000);
    };

    function oneInput(){

        $(this).donetyping(function(callback){

            var importe_parse = parseFloat($('#importe').val().replace(/[.\/#!$%\^&\*;:{}=\-_`~()]/g,''));

            if(!isNaN(importe_parse)){

                if ($('#importe').val().length > 0){
                    $('#calculadora-search').request('onCalculadora', {
                        data:{
                            moneda_origen: $('#moneda_origen').val(),
                            importe: importe_parse,
                            moneda_destino: $('#moneda_destino').val(),
                            search: '0',
                        },
                    });

                    loader_gif.removeClass('hidden');
                    loader_gif.addClass('active');
                    o_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
                    d_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
                    $('#importe').prop('disabled', true);
                    $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', true);

                    setTimeout(function(){
                        loader_gif.removeClass('active');
                        loader_gif.addClass('hidden');
                        o_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
                        d_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
                        $('#importe').prop('disabled', false);
                        $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', false);
                    }, 2000);
                }
            }else {

                const Toast = Swal.mixin({
                    toast: true,
                    position: 'top-end',
                    showConfirmButton: false,
                    timer: 3000
                });

                Toast.fire({
                    type: 'error',
                    title: 'Ingrese un valor numerico'
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function twoInput(){
        $(this).donetyping(function(callback){

            var segundo_valor_parse = parseFloat($('#segundo_valor').val().replace(/[.\/#!$%\^&\*;:{}=\-_`~()]/g,''));

            if(!isNaN(segundo_valor_parse)){

                if ($('#segundo_valor').val().length > 0){
                    $('#calculadora-search').request('onCalculadora', {
                        data:{
                            moneda_origen: $('#moneda_origen').val(),
                            segundo_valor: segundo_valor_parse,
                            moneda_destino: $('#moneda_destino').val(),
                            search: '1',
                        },
                    });

                    loader_gif.removeClass('hidden');
                    loader_gif.addClass('active');
                    o_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
                    d_moneda.prop('disabled', 'disabled');
                    $('#importe').prop('disabled', true);
                    $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', true);

                    setTimeout(function(){
                        loader_gif.removeClass('active');
                        loader_gif.addClass('hidden');
                        o_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
                        d_moneda.prop('disabled', false);
                        $('#importe').prop('disabled', false);
                        $("#segundo_valor").prop('disabled', false);
                    }, 2000);
                }
            }else {
                $(window).on("load", function(){
                    const Toast = Swal.mixin({
                        toast: true,
                        position: 'top-end',
                        showConfirmButton: false,
                        timer: 3000
                    })

                    Toast.fire({
                        type: 'error',
                        title: 'Ingrese un valor numerico'
                    })
                });
            }
        });
    }

</script>    </body>

</html>
